| ------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `object`                                                |
| **Required**              | No                                                      |
| **Additional properties** | [[Not allowed]](# "Additional Properties not allowed.") |

| Property                                 | Pattern | Type             | Deprecated | Definition | Title/Description                      |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------- | ---------------- | ---------- | ---------- | -------------------------------------- |
| + [$schema](#$schema )                   | No      | string           | No         | -          | -                                      |
| + [version](#version )                   | No      | enum (of string) | No         | -          | -                                      |
| + [scenario](#scenario )                 | No      | enum (of string) | No         | -          | The general scenario of this data file |
| - [specimens](#specimens )               | No      | array            | No         | -          | -                                      |
| - [probes](#probes )                     | No      | array            | No         | -          | -                                      |
| - [wedges](#wedges )                     | No      | array of object  | No         | -          | -                                      |
| - [acquisitionUnits](#acquisitionUnits ) | No      | array of object  | No         | -          | -                                      |

| - [dataEncodings](#dataEncodings )       | No      | array of object  | No         | -          | -                                      |
| + [groups](#groups )                     | No      | array of object  | No         | -          | -                                      |

## <a name="$schema"></a>1. Property `root > $schema`

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | Yes      |

| Restrictions   |   |
| -------------- | - |
| **Min length** | 1 |

## <a name="version"></a>2. Property `root > version`

|              |                    |
| ------------ | ------------------ |
| **Type**     | `enum (of string)` |
| **Required** | Yes                |

Must be one of:
* "3.1.0"

## <a name="scenario"></a>3. Property `root > scenario`

|              |                    |
| ------------ | ------------------ |
| **Type**     | `enum (of string)` |
| **Required** | Yes                |

**Description:** The general scenario of this data file

Must be one of:
* "General Weld"
* "General Mapping"

### <a name="autogenerated_heading_17"></a>6.1. root > wedges > wedges items

##### <a name="groups_items_dataset_storageMode"></a>10.1.14.1. Property `root > groups > groups items > dataset > storageMode`
